NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

[Part VI—Sec. 4

PUBLIC NOTICES
R.R. BASKARAN, S/o. late Thiru. R.R. RAMALINGAM, residing at No. 8A, Balarengapuram 1st Cross Street,
Madurai-09, have adopted P.G Venkatesh Babu, born on 09-02-1997, to biological parents late Gnanasekaran
and late Neelavathy.
This adoption is made vide Court Order O.S. No. 426/2014, wherein the District Sessions Court Judge has pronounced
P.G Venkatesh Babu as my adopted son, and so he shall henceforth be known as R.B. VENKATESH BABU.
Madurai,
1st October 2015.

R.R. BASKARAN.
(Adoptive Father.)

R.R. BASKARAN, S/o. late Thiru. R.R. RAMALINGAM, residing at No. 8A, Balarengapuram 1st Cross Street,
Madurai-09, have adopted P.G. Karthick, born on 27-09-1994, to biological parents late Gnanasekaran and late Neelavathy.
This adoption is made vide Court Order O.S. No. 426/2014, wherein the District Sessions Court Judge has pronounced
P.G Karthick as my adopted son, and so he shall henceforth be known as R.B. KARTHICK.
Madurai,
1st October 2015.

R.R. BASKARAN,
(Adoptive Father.)
